For each player, each row is a different game with these columns:
oppid: Opponent's AGA ID
result: +/- for win or loss, my color, handicap
pre: Opp Rating before event
dec: Opponent's declared rank
dur: Opponent's effective starting rating, based on pre-rating and declared rank
post: Opponent's final rating after the event
tourney: Tournament this game is part of
